Actor RedVixen : BlueVixen {
	Health 2000
	Tag "Alien Vixen"
    States
    {
    Spawn:
		RR25 E 0
		RR25 E 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
		RR25 E 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
		RR25 E 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
	Spawn2:
		RR25 A 0 A_JumpIfinventory("VixenTaunt",1,2)
		RR25 E 4 A_Look
		loop
		RR25 I 0 A_SetShootable 
		RR25 I 0 A_SetTranslucent(1,0) 
		RR25 IJKL 3 A_Look
		RR25 A 0 A_PlaySound("Vixen/Laugh")	
		RR25 MNO 3 A_Look
		RR25 IJKLMNO 3 A_Look
		RR25 A 0 A_TakeInventory("VixenTaunt",1)
		RR25 IJKLMNO 3 A_Look
		RR25 IJKLMNO 3 A_Look
		loop
	Idle:
		RR25 I 0 A_SetTranslucent(1,0) 
		RR25 A 0 A_JumpIfinventory("VixenTaunt",1,2)
		RR25 E 4 A_Look
		loop
		RR25 I 0 A_SetShootable 
		RR25 IJKL 3 A_Look
		RR25 A 0 A_PlaySound("Vixen/Laugh")	
		RR25 MNO 3 A_Look
		RR25 IJKLMNO 3 A_Look

		RR25 IJKLMNO 3 A_Look

    See:
		RR25 A 0 A_GiveInventory("VixenTaunt",1)

		Loop

    Missile:
		RR25 A 0 A_Jump(50,"TeleBitch") //Just go to the teleport state
		RR25 A 0 A_Jump(78,"BraFire") //Jump to Alien Teat Gun attack

Actor GreenVixen : BlueVixen {
	Health 500
	Tag "Alien Vixen"
    States
    {
    Spawn:
		RR22 E 0
		RR22 E 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
		RR22 E 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
		RR22 E 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
	Spawn2:
		RR22 A 0 A_JumpIfinventory("VixenTaunt",1,2)
		RR22 E 4 A_Look
		loop
		RR22 I 0 A_SetShootable 
		RR22 I 0 A_SetTranslucent(1,0) 
		RR22 IJKL 3 A_Look
		RR22 A 0 A_PlaySound("Vixen/Laugh")	
		RR22 MNO 3 A_Look
		RR22 IJKLMNO 3 A_Look
		RR22 A 0 A_TakeInventory("VixenTaunt",1)
		RR22 IJKLMNO 3 A_Look
		RR22 IJKLMNO 3 A_Look
		loop
	Idle:
		RR22 I 0 A_SetTranslucent(1,0) 
		RR22 A 0 A_JumpIfinventory("VixenTaunt",1,2)
		RR22 E 4 A_Look
		loop
		RR22 I 0 A_SetShootable 
		RR22 IJKL 3 A_Look
		RR22 A 0 A_PlaySound("Vixen/Laugh")	
		RR22 MNO 3 A_Look
		RR22 IJKLMNO 3 A_Look
		RR22 A 0 A_TakeInventory("VixenTaunt",1)
		RR22 IJKLMNO 3 A_Look
		RR22 IJKLMNO 3 A_Look
		loop	
    See:
		RR22 A 0 A_GiveInventory("VixenTaunt",1)
	FuckSee:
		RR22 ABCDEFGH 4 A_Chase
		RR22 A 0 A_Jump(10,"TeleBitch")
		Loop

		RR21 I 0 A_PlaySound("Vixen/TeleIn")

		RR21 L 6 A_SetTranslucent(0.7,1)
		RR21 KJI 6 A_SetTranslucent(1,0)
		RR21 I 0 A_SetShootable	
		Goto FuckSee
    Missile:
		RR22 A 0 A_Jump(50,"TeleBitch") //Just go to the teleport state
		RR22 A 0 A_Jump(78,"BraFire") //Jump to Alien Teat Gun attack

		RR22 Q 5 A_CustomMissile("VixenBlast",46,0,0)

Actor BrownVixen : BlueVixen {
	Health 750
	Tag "Alien Vixen"
    States
    {
    Spawn:
		RR19 E 0
		RR19 E 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"Spawn2")
		RR19 E 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
		RR19 E 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
	Spawn2:
		RR19 A 0 A_JumpIfinventory("VixenTaunt",1,2)
		RR19 E 4 A_Look
		loop
		RR19 I 0 A_SetShootable 
		RR19 I 0 A_SetTranslucent(1,0) 
		RR19 IJKL 3 A_Look

		RR19 IJKLMNO 3 A_Look
		RR19 A 0 A_TakeInventory("VixenTaunt",1)
		RR19 IJKLMNO 3 A_Look
		RR19 IJKLMNO 3 A_Look
		loop
	Idle:
		RR19 I 0 A_SetTranslucent(1,0) 
		RR19 A 0 A_JumpIfinventory("VixenTaunt",1,2)
		RR19 E 4 A_Look
		loop
		RR19 I 0 A_SetShootable 
		RR19 IJKL 3 A_Look
		RR19 A 0 A_PlaySound("Vixen/Laugh")	
		RR19 MNO 3 A_Look
		RR19 IJKLMNO 3 A_Look

    See:

    Missile:

	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:

		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)

	}

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))

actor SpecialVixen_Shrink : SpecialVixen
{

		See:

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			RR28 E 4 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			RR28 F 4 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			RR28 G 4 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			RR28 H 4 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SpecialVixen", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_DamageChildren(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker",2))
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}
}

Actor Vixenblast
{
    radius 4
    height 6
    scale 0.15
    damage 5
    speed 30
	+STRIFEDAMAGE
	DONTHURTSHOOTER
    deathsound "rr/rico1"
	DamageType "Explosive"
    +MISSILE
    PROJECTILE
    states
    {
    Spawn:
		VIX2 QRS 4 Bright
		loop
	Crash:
	Death:
		CH_R R 2 Bright A_Explode(18,4)
		CH_R SSTTUUVVWWXXYYZZ 1 Bright
		CH_7 AABBCCDDEEFFGGHHIIJJKKL 1 Bright
		CH_7 LL 1 Bright A_FadeOut	
		stop
    }
}
